---
sidebar_position: 5
title: Printcart Webhooks
---

You can use webhook subscriptions to receive notifications about particular events in a shop. After you've subscribed to a webhook topic, your app can execute code immediately after specific events occur in shops that have your app installed, instead of having to make API calls periodically to check their status.

For example, you can rely on a webhook to trigger an action in your app when a new product or order arrives.By using webhooks, you can make fewer API calls overall, which makes sure that your apps are more efficient and update quickly.

For more information on how to create a webhook and the data returned by the event topic, refer to the [Webhook API](/rest-api-reference#tag/Webhook) and the [Webhook event topic](/docs/api-sdk/webhooks#event-topics)

## The Webhook subscription object

### Properties

#### <span style={{ color: `var(--ifm-color-primary)` }}>`callback_url`</span> {#callback_url}

Destination URI to which the webhook subscription should send the `POST` request when an event occurs.

#### <span style={{ color: `var(--ifm-color-primary)` }}>`created_at`</span> {#created_at}

Date and time when the webhook subscription was created. The API returns this value in

#### <span style={{ color: `var(--ifm-color-primary)` }}>`event`</span> {#event}

Event that triggers the webhook.

#### <span style={{ color: `var(--ifm-color-primary)` }}>`id`</span> {#id}

Unique identifier string for webhook registration.

#### <span style={{ color: `var(--ifm-color-primary)` }}>`topic`</span> {#topic}

Topic for webhook registration

#### <span style={{ color: `var(--ifm-color-primary)` }}>`updated_at`</span> {#updated_at}

Date and time when the webhook subscription was updated. The API returns this value in

## Webhook event topics {#event-topics}

### Designs {#Designs}

<details>
  <summary>
    <b>Create</b>
  </summary>
  <div>
    <div>
      <p>Occurs whenever a design is created.</p>
      <p>
        Resource: <a href="/rest-api-reference/#tag/Design/operation/getDesignById">Design</a>
      </p>
    </div>
  </div>

<details>
  <summary>
    <b>Update</b>
  </summary>
  <div>
    <div>
      <p>Occurs whenever a design is updated.</p>
      <p>
        Resource: <a href="/rest-api-reference/#tag/Design/operation/getDesignById">Design</a>
      </p>
    </div>
  </div>

<details>
  <summary>
    <b>Update Batch</b>
  </summary>
  <div>
    <div>
      <p>Occurs whenever a designs is updated batch.</p>
      <p>
        Resource: <a href="/rest-api-reference/#tag/Design/operation/getDesignById">Design</a>

  <summary>
    <b>Delete Batch</b>
  </summary>
  <div>
    <div>
      <p>Occurs whenever a designs is deleted batch.</p>
      <p>
        Resource: <a href="/rest-api-reference/#tag/Design/operation/getDesignById">Design</a>

### Products {#Products}

<details>
  <summary>
    <b>Create</b>
  </summary>
  <div>
    <div>
      <p>Occurs whenever a product is created.</p>
      <p>Resource: <a href='/rest-api-reference/#tag/Product/operation/getProductByID'>Product</a></p>
      <p>Payload:</p>
    </div>
  </div>

```json
  {
    "data": {
      {
        "id": "f95fxxx-6cc1-4f24-8a60-e1be1242xxx",
        "name": "Custom Product",
        "status": "publish",
        "dynamic_side": false,
        "viewport_width": null,
        "viewport_height": null,
        "scale": null,
        "dpi": 72,
        "allowed_file_types": [
            "jpg",
            "png"
        ],
        "max_file_upload": 1,
        "min_jpg_dpi": 96,
        "dimension_unit": "cm",
        "enable_design": false,
        "enable_upload": false,
        "upload_max_filesize": 50,
        "integration_product_id": null,
        "product_image": {
            "id": "0c49xxxx-d2ca-4aec-9cc1-ded6221xxxxx",
            "name": "example-image.jpg",
            "url": "https://dcisb67tbokpv.cloudfront.net/images/f95fxxx-6cc1-4f24-8a60-e1be1242xxx/dbYExswRzxihgbka1sbn7mTOmdA6TqSLYDxxxxxx.jpg",
            "thumbnails": null,
            "alt": null,
            "width": 600,
            "height": 600,
            "created_at": "2023-03-12T09:20:03.000000Z",
            "updated_at": "2023-03-12T09:20:03.000000Z"
        },
        "created_at": "2023-03-12T09:20:18.000000Z",
        "updated_at": "2023-03-12T09:20:58.000000Z"
      }
    },
    "message": "Created successfully",
  }
```

</details>

<details>
  <summary>
    <b>Update</b>
  </summary>
  <div>
    <div>
      <p>Occurs whenever a product is updated.</p>
      <p>Resource: <a href='/rest-api-reference/#tag/Product/operation/getProductByID'>Product</a></p>
    </div>
  </div>

```json
  {
    "data": {
      {
        "id": "f95fxxx-6cc1-4f24-8a60-e1be1242xxx",
        "name": "Update Product",
        "status": "publish",
        "dynamic_side": false,
        "viewport_width": null,
        "viewport_height": null,
        "scale": null,
        "dpi": 72,
        "allowed_file_types": [
            "jpg",
            "png"
        ],
        "max_file_upload": 1,
        "min_jpg_dpi": 96,
        "dimension_unit": "cm",
        "enable_design": false,
        "enable_upload": false,
        "upload_max_filesize": 50,
        "integration_product_id": null,
        "product_image": {
```

### Templates {#Template}

<details>
  <summary>
    <b>Create</b>
  </summary>
  <div>
    <div>
      <p>Occurs whenever a template is created.</p>
      <p>Resource: <a href="/rest-api-reference/#tag/Template/operation/getTemplateById">Template</a></p>
    </div>
  </div>

```json
{
  "data": {
    "id": "cce4dc71-6757-4a1c-a259-6b66a4304c14",
    "note": "Template example note",
    "side": {
      "type": null,
      "id": "c5661a1e-8147-4dc3-8600-00fdc81ed14b",
      "name": "Side Example",
      "ratio": 72,
      "dimension_unit": "cm",
      "status": "publish",
      "design_area": {
        "width": 50,
        "height": 50,
        "top": 50,
        "left": 50
      },
      "show_cut_line": true,
      "cut_line_margin": {
        "x": 50.5,
        "y": 50.5
      },
      "show_safe_zone": true,
      "safe_zone_margin": {
        "x": 50.5,
        "y": 50.5
      },
      "side_image_size": {
        "width": 50,
        "height": 50
```

<details>
  <summary>
    <b>Delete</b>
  </summary>
  <div>
    <div>
      <p>Occurs whenever a template is deleted.</p>
      <p>Resource: <a href="/rest-api-reference/#tag/Template/operation/getTemplateById">Template</a></p>
    </div>
  </div>

<details>
  <summary>
    <b>Create Batch</b>
  </summary>
  <div>
    <div>
      <p>Occurs whenever a templates is created batch.</p>
      <p>Resource: <a href="/rest-api-reference/#tag/Template/operation/getTemplateById">Template</a></p>
    </div>
  </div>

<details>
  <summary>
    <b>Update Batch</b>
  </summary>
  <div>
    <div>
      <p>Occurs whenever a templates is updated batch.</p>
      <p>Resource: <a href="/rest-api-reference/#tag/Template/operation/getTemplateById">Template</a></p>
    </div>
  </div>

<details>
  <summary>
    <b>Delete Batch</b>
  </summary>
  <div>
    <div>
      <p>Occurs whenever a templates is deleted batch.</p>
      <p>Resource: <a href="/rest-api-reference/#tag/Template/operation/getTemplateById">Template</a></p>
    </div>
  </div>
